	template <typename T>
	:ref:`Ptr<doxid-d2/d56/structcv_1_1_ptr>`<T>
	:ref:`makePtr<doxid-dc/d84/group__core__basic_1ga94b059075f41314c83dd2a2758c81acd>`();
